style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司将购买取得<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>70%</SPAN>的股权作为长期股权投资入账的会计处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：长期股权投资——<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司 （<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2.95</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>5 000</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US>14 750 
</SPAN>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：股本<SPAN lang=EN-US> 5 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>资本公积<SPAN lang=EN-US> 9 
750<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>）调整子公司资产和负债的公允价值。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>编制购买日的合并资产负债表时，根据<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司购买<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司设置的股权备查簿中登记的信息，将<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司资产和负债的评估增值或减值分别调增或调减相关资产和负债项目的金额。根据税法规定，在购买日子公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司的资产和负债的计税基础还是其原来的账面价值。购买日子公司资产和负债的公允价值与其计税基础之间的差异，形成暂时性差异。在符合有关原则和确认条件的情况下，编制购买日合并财务报表时，需要对该暂时性差异确认相应的递延所得税资产或递延所得税负债。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>本例中，<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司应收账款的公允价值低于其计税基础的金额为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>400 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 960-1 
560</SPAN>），形成可抵扣暂时性差异，应当对其确认递延所得税资产<SPAN lang=EN-US>100 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>400</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>25%</SPAN>）；存货的公允价值高于其计税基础的金额为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 000 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>11 000</SPAN>－<SPAN lang=EN-US>10 
000</SPAN>），形成应纳税暂时性差异，应当对其确认递延所得税负债<SPAN lang=EN-US>250 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 000</SPAN>×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>25%</SPAN>）；固定资产中的办公楼的公允价值高于其计税基础的金额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>3 000 
</SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 000</SPAN>－<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 
000</SPAN>），形成应纳税暂时性差异，应当对其确认递延所得税负债<SPAN lang=EN-US>750 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>3 000</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>25%</SPAN>）。在合并工作底稿中的调整分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：存货<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 000 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>固定资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 3 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>递延所得税资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
100<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：应收账款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
400<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>递延所得税负债 （<SPAN lang=EN-US>250+750</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>资本公积<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 
700<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">2. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">母公司长期股权投资与子公司所有者权益的抵销处理。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>经过对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司资产和负债的公允价值调整后，<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司所有者权益总额＝<SPAN lang=EN-US>16 000</SPAN>＋<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 
700=18 700</SPAN>（万元），<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司所有者权益中拥有的份额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 090 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>18 
700</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>70%</SPAN>），<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司对<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司长期股权投资的金额为<SPAN lang=EN-US>14 750 </SPAN>万元，因此合并商誉为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1 660 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>14 750-13 090</SPAN>）。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司购买<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司股权所形成的商誉，在<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司个别财务报表中表示对<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司长期股权投资的一部分，在编制合并财务报表时，将长期股权投资与在子公司所有者权益中所拥有的份额相抵销，其抵销差额在合并资产负债表中则表现为商誉。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司长期股权投资与其在<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司所有者权益中拥有份额的抵销分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：股本<SPAN lang=EN-US> 10 000 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>3</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>资本公积<SPAN lang=EN-US> 6 
700<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>盈余公积<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
600<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>未分配利润<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 
400<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>商誉<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 
660<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：长期股权投资——<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US> 14 
750<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>少数股东权益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 5 
610<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>需要注意的是，母子公司有交互持股情形的，在编制合并财务报表时，对于母公司持有的子公司股权，与通常情况下母公司长期股权投资与子公司所有者权益的合并抵销处理相同。对于子公司持有的母公司股权，应当按照子公司取得母公司股权日所确认的长期股权投资的初始投资成本，将其转为合并财务报表中的库存股；对于子公司持有母公司股权所确认的投资收益（如利润分配或现金股利），应当进行抵销处理。子公司将所持有的母公司股权分类为可供出售金融资产的，按照公允价值计量的，同时冲销子公司累计确认的公允价值变动。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">3. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">编制购买日合并资产负债表工作底稿及合并资产负债表。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>根据上述调整分录和抵销分录，<SPAN lang=EN-US>A 
</SPAN>公司编制购买日合并资产负债表工作底稿见表<SPAN lang=EN-US>3</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>根据上述合并资产负债表工作底稿中各项目的合并金额，编制购买日的合并资产负债表（略）。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%"><SPAN lang=EN-US

style="mso-no-proof: yes"></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（三）购买日后合并财务报表的编制<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>根据本准则规定，母公司应当以自身和其子公司的财务报表为基础，根据其他有关资料，编制合并财务报表。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司和<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>31 </SPAN>日资产负债表见表<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>4</SPAN>：<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>表<SPAN lang=EN-US>4 <SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN>资产负债表（简表） 
会企<SPAN lang=EN-US>01 </SPAN>表<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>

<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN

<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US

</SPAN><SPAN

</SPAN>年度利润表见表<SPAN lang=EN-US>5</SPAN>：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-no-proof: yes"></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US

<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司和<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年度现金流量表见表<SPAN lang=EN-US>6</SPAN>：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>表<SPAN lang=EN-US>6 </SPAN>现金流量表（简表） 会企<SPAN lang=EN-US>03 
</SPAN>表<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>编制单位：<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>/B 
</SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 </SPAN>年度 单位：万元<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>项目<SPAN lang=EN-US> A</SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
B</SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-no-proof: yes"></SPAN><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;（图略）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-no-proof: yes"></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司和<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年度所有者权益变动表见表<SPAN lang=EN-US>7</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-no-proof: yes"></SPAN><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;（图略）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-no-proof: yes"></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">1. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">对母子公司个别财务报表的调整处理。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>）调整子公司资产和负债的公允价值。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>根据<SPAN lang=EN-US>A </SPAN>公司购买<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司设置的股权备查簿中登记的信息，将<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司资产和负债的评估增值或减值分别调增或调减相关资产和负债项目的金额。在合并工作底稿中的调整分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：存货<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 000 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>固定资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 3 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>递延所得税资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
100<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：应付账款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
400<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>递延所得税负债 （<SPAN lang=EN-US>250+750</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>资本公积<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 
700<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>）根据子公司已实现的公允价值调整当期净利润。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>本例中，合并财务报表要求以子公司资产、负债的公允价值为基础进行确认，而子公司个别财务报表是按其资产、负债的原账面价值为基础编制的，其当期计算的净利润也是以其资产、负债的原账面价值为基础计算的结果。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>因此，上述公允价值与原账面价值存在差额的资产或负债项目，在经营过程中因资产的折旧、摊销和减值等对子公司当期净利润的影响，需要在净利润计算中予以反映。在合并财务报表工作底稿中的调整分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：营业成本<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 000 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>管理费用<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
200<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>应收账款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
400<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：存货<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 
000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>固定资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
200<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>资产减值损失<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
400<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>因此，经已实现公允价值调整后的<SPAN lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 </SPAN>年度净利润<SPAN lang=EN-US>=5 
250</SPAN>＋<SPAN lang=EN-US>400</SPAN>（因购买日应收账款公允价值减值的实现而调减资产减值损失）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>-1 000</SPAN>（因购买日存货公允价值增值的实现而调增营业成本）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>-200</SPAN>（因固定资产公允价值增值计算的折旧而调增管理费用）<SPAN lang=EN-US>=4 
450</SPAN>（万元）。<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>3</SPAN>）递延所得税资产或递延所得税负债的暂时性差异的转回。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>由于<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司应收账款按购买日评估的确认的金额已收回，评估确认的坏账已核销，因递延所得税资产的转回而增加当期所得税费用<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>100 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>400</SPAN>×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>25%</SPAN>）；由于<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司购买日发生评估增值的存货当年已全部实现对外销售，因递延所得税负债的转回而减少当期所得税费用<SPAN lang=EN-US>250 
</SPAN>万元（<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 000</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>25%</SPAN>）；由于<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司购买日发生增值的办公楼<SPAN lang=EN-US>2</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>13 
</SPAN>年年末应纳税暂时性差异为<SPAN lang=EN-US>2 800 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>3000-200</SPAN>）应确认的递延所得税负债为<SPAN lang=EN-US>700 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2 800</SPAN>×<SPAN lang=EN-US>25%</SPAN>），因递延所得税负债的转回而减少当期所得税费用<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>50 </SPAN>万元（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>750-700</SPAN>）。在合并财务报表工作底稿中的调整分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：递延所得税负债 （<SPAN lang=EN-US>250+50</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>300 </SPAN>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>3</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>

lang=EN-US>200</SPAN>）。<SPAN

000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>——本年利润分配<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 
250<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>——年末<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 
800<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>7</SPAN>）抵销应收账款与应付账款项目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>在合并财务报表工作底稿中的抵销分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：应付账款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 500 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>7</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：应收账款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
500<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>8</SPAN>）抵销坏账准备与资产减值损失项目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司将与<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司往来的内部应收账款与应付账款相互抵销的同时，还应将内部应收账款计提的坏账准备予以抵销。在合并财务报表工作底稿中的抵销分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：应收账款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 20 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>8</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：资产减值损失<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
20<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>需要注意的是，在连续编制合并财务报表时，对于内部应收款项及其坏账准备，应当按照如下程序进行合并处理：首先，将内部应收款项与应付款项予以抵销，按照内部应付款项的数额，借记“应付账款”、“应付票据”等项目，贷记“应收账款”、“应收票据”等项目；其次，应将上期资产减值损失中抵销的各内部应收款项计提的相应坏账准备对本期期初未分配利润的影响予以抵销，按照上期资产减值损失项目中抵销的各内部应收款项计提的相应坏账准备的数额，借记“应收账款”等项目，贷记“未分配利润——期初”项目；最后，对于本期各内部应收款项在个别财务报表中补提或者冲销的相应坏账准备的数额也应予以抵销，按照本期期末内部应收款项在个别资产负债表中补提（或冲销）的坏账准备的数额，借记（或贷记）“应收账款”等项目，贷记（或借记）“资产减值损失”项目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>9</SPAN>）抵销因抵销坏账准备与资产减值损失产生的所得税影响。在合并财务报表工作底稿中的抵销分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：所得税费用 （<SPAN lang=EN-US>20</SPAN>×<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>25%</SPAN>）<SPAN lang=EN-US>5 </SPAN>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>9</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：递延所得税资产<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
5<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>10</SPAN>）抵销应收股利与应付股利项目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">A 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">公司根据<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>B </SPAN>公司宣告分派现金股利的公告，按照其所享有的金额已确认应收股利，并在其资产负债表中计列应收股利<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1575 </SPAN>万元。在合并财务报表工作底稿中的抵销分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：应付股利<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 575 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>10</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：应收股利<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 
575<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=3><FONT face=宋体><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">3. 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">抵销内部顺流交易的存货<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>11</SPAN>）抵销内部销售收入、成本和内部销售形成的存货价值中包含的未实现内部销售损益。在合并财务报表工作底稿中的抵销分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：营业收入<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 000 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>11</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：营业成本<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
700<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>存货<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
300<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>需要注意的是，在连续编制合并财务报表时，对于内部销售存货，应当按照如下程序进行合并处理：首先，将上期抵销的存货价值中包含的未实现内部损益对本期期初未分配利润的影响进行抵销，按照上期内部购入存货价值中包含的未实现内部销售损益的数额，借记“未分配利润——期初”项目，贷记“营业成本”项目；其次，对于本期发生的内部销售存货，将内部销售收入、内部销售成本及内部购入存货中未实现内部销售损益予以抵销，按照销售企业内部销售收入的数额，借记“营业收入”项目，贷记“营业成本”项目；最后，将期末内部购入存货价值中包含的未实现内部销售损益予以抵销，对于期末内部销售形成的存货（包括上期结转形成的本期存货），应当按照购买企业期末内部购入存货价值中包含的未实现内部销售损益的数额，借记“营业成本”项目，贷记“存货”项目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>（<SPAN lang=EN-US>12</SPAN>）抵销<SPAN lang=EN-US>B 
</SPAN>公司本期计提的存货跌价准备。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>在合并财务报表工作底稿中的抵销分录如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>借：存货<SPAN lang=EN-US> 20 </SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>12</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT face=宋体>贷：资产减值损失<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
20<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>需要注意的是，在连续编制合并财务报表时，对于内部销售存货的存货跌价准备，应当按照如下程序进行合并处理：首先，将上期资产减值损失中抵销的存货跌价准备对本期期初未分配利润的影响予以抵销，按照上期资产减值损失项目中抵销的存货跌价准备的数额，借记“存货”项目，贷记“未分配利润——期初”项目；其次，对于本期对内部购入存货在个别财务报表中补提（或冲销）的存货跌价准备的数额也应予以抵销，按照本期对内部购入存货在个别财务报表中补提（或冲销）的存货跌价准备的数额，借记（或贷记）“存货”项目，贷记（或借记）“资产减值损失”项目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
size=3><FONT 
face=宋体>对于抵销存货跌价准备的数额，应当分别下列不同情况进行处理：当本期内部购入存货的可变现净值低于持有该存货企业的取得成本但高于抵销未实现内部销售损益后的取得成本（即销售企业对该存货的取得成本）时，其抵销的存货跌价准备的金额为本期存货跌价准备的增加额；当本期内部购入存货的可变现净值低于抵销未实现内部销售损益后的取得成本（即销售企业对该存货的取得成本）时，其抵销的存货跌价准备的金额为相对于购买企业该存货的取得成本高于销售企业取得成本的差额部分计提的跌价准备的数额扣除期初内部购入存货计提的存货跌价准备的金额后的余额，即本期期末存货中包含的未实现内部销售损益的金额减去期初内部购入存货计提的存货跌价准备的金额后的余额。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 180%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT
